The Tragic Bloodshed Involving Housewife and Maid – Suspect Luo Yusheng and Luo Yefu Arrested – Blood Stains Found Inside the Hem of Luo's Western-Style Trousers – Two Boxes of Valuables Stored at a Friend's House – Luo Initially Confessed to the Murder During Interrogation but Completely Denied It During Court Trial Yesterday Morning 122

Mrs. Jin Dai, a woman from Jinhua, Zhejiang Province (also known as Jin Baozhen), residing at 459, third floor, Erjin Road, North Henan Road, and her maid, Luo, were suddenly attacked by an intruder around 8 AM on the 23rd of this month. Both women were fatally wounded with axes. Hua Detective Shang Wu, Detectives Zhao Qingkui and Bao Langchun from the Huishi Police Department, and Western Detective Shamboro, apprehended Luo Yusheng, a native of Yiwu, Zhejiang (age 21, residing at 31 Xinqiao Road, Nanshi), as the suspect in the case.

(Currently serving as the Director of Studies at Mingchen Elementary School and also the son of lawyer Luo Zhaoxin, who was fatally shot on Guangdong Road, Qinghefang, on June 19th of last year.) He was taken into custody at the police station and escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court yesterday morning at 9:30 AM. Judge Liu Yugui presided over the interrogation, and the defendant, Luo Yusheng, was represented by lawyer Lou Yunmei. The trial lasted approximately three hours. Due to the need for further investigation in the case, the trial was postponed for seven days for further review. A detailed account of the

Trial Proceedings is as follows: First, Police Barrister Zhang Tianyin stated that the police department is prosecuting the defendant Luo Yusheng for murder under Article 271 of the criminal law. At 10:40 AM on the 23rd of this month, the police department received a phone report stating that two women had been murdered at 459, third floor, North Henan Road. The police department immediately dispatched an ambulance and rushed the injured to Shanghai Sanitarium on Lao Bazi Road. However, Jin Dai passed away due to her serious injuries before arriving at the hospital.

The maid, Luo, suffered four axe wounds to the face and two to the head, and her injuries were also severe. She died at the hospital at 2:30 PM that afternoon, and her body was sent to the coroner's office for examination. After the inspection by the prosecutor's office of the court, the police department dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to the scene to conduct a detailed investigation. They found Jin Dai lying on the sofa in the front room and Luo lying on the floor, both covered in blood. There was a significant amount of blood on the floor. Next to Luo's body, they found

an Axe. Another axe was found under the bed in the back room. At that time, Jin Yongren, son of the deceased Jin Dai, and her daughter, Jin Lingyi, reported to the detectives that important items that their mother had kept in the bedside cabinet, such as the passbook with the Tongyuan Bank's Jin Ji account name, etc., were missing. In addition to finding a tram ticket of 12 points next to the cabinet, the detectives also learned that Jin had a safety deposit box at the Shanghai Bank. Therefore, based on

this clue, they rushed to the Shanghai Bank to investigate. However, in order to comply with banking practices, the bank refused to disclose the contents of the safe deposit box, only stating that a person had recently come with a key to open the box and described the person's age, appearance, and clothing. Upon hearing this, the deceased's daughter, Jin Lingyi, immediately declared to the detectives that, based on the person's age and accent, it was Luo Yusheng, her fellow townsman who worked as a teacher at Mingchen Elementary School. The detectives, together with police detectives from the Public Security Bureau, went to Mingchen Elementary School at 31 Xinqiao Road, Nanshi, to arrest the defendant. They found 100 yuan in banknotes and 17 yuan in small change in his suitcase, as well as a pair of western-style trousers. The trousers appeared to have been recently washed but were not yet dry, and the inside of the trouser legs had

a lot of blood stains. He was then taken to the Public Security Bureau and brought back to the police station at 10:40 AM yesterday morning for questioning. At first, he denied everything. Later, Wang Mingrong, residing at 14 Jiu'an Lane, Huangjiaque Road, Nanshi, saw the news of Luo Yusheng's arrest in the newspaper and suddenly remembered that Luo had left two leather suitcases at Wang's place on the morning of the 23rd. In order to disassociate himself, Wang sent the two leather suitcases left by Luo to the Municipal Public Security Bureau. Upon opening the suitcases, they were found to contain valuable items and

Jin Lingyi's seals, and three of her personal seals. Upon receiving this information, Chief Detective Shang led Jin Lingyi to identify the items in the suitcases. All the items were confirmed to belong to her mother. The two suitcases are currently stored at the Public Security Bureau. Chief Detective Shang then interrogated the defendant severely. The defendant finally confessed the truth, stating that his father, Luo Zhaoxin, was a lawyer in Ningbo and had a close relationship with Jin Zhaozong, the former Chief Prosecutor of the Ningbo District Court (the deceased's husband). Later, Luo Zhaoxin was

shot and killed in Qinghefang, Shanghai, last year. Jin Dai was in charge of a lot of money and property. The defendant, unable to obtain anything, harbored resentment and sought revenge. On August of this year, after the defendant took over Mingchen Elementary School, lawyer Lou Yunmei, who is now defending the defendant, introduced Xu Wenxian to the school as a tea server. The defendant then conspired with Xu to plan the revenge. Xu invited a Mr. Ma, and at 7:00 AM on the 23rd, the defendant took the Route 6 tram in the French Concession and then transferred to the Route 14

Trolleybus, arriving directly at the intersection of North Henan Road and Lao Bazi Road. At that time, Xu and Ma were already waiting at the station with axes. After meeting, they waited around because it was still early and Jin Dai's children had not yet gone to school. Around 8:00 AM, the defendant led them to Jin's house. The defendant stood guard downstairs while Xu and Ma went upstairs with axes. Shortly after, Xu and the others came downstairs, saying that the matter had been settled. The defendant then went upstairs, opened the bedside cabinet, took out the bank passbook and the safety deposit box key, and returned to school by tram.

In his haste, he left a tram ticket upstairs in the deceased's house. Later, Xu also returned to school and told the defendant that he had been given a reward of 50 yuan. He also claimed that he had stolen the Shanghai Bank safe deposit box key before going upstairs, secretly carved a seal, went to the Shanghai Bank to open the box, and obtained a lot of property. He packed it together with the items taken from Jin's house that day into two suitcases and transported them to the house he had rented on Huangjiaque Road (monthly rent of 12 yuan), etc. After obtaining the confession, the detectives took the defendant to the

Scene of the crime to demonstrate what happened at the time. Currently, this case is requesting a postponement in order to apprehend the accomplices. Furthermore, the blood stains on the western-style trousers seized from the defendant's school are currently being analyzed by the Chemistry Department of the Public Works Bureau to determine if they are the same as the deceased's blood. Also, two official letters are requested, one to the Shanghai Bank, ordering them to fully explain the contents of Jin Dai's safety deposit box to the police department for reference, and one to the Public Security Bureau, requesting that

the two suitcases be transferred for investigation, etc. Then, the axe and the photographs taken at the scene were presented as evidence. Subsequently, Jin Yongren, son of Jin Dai, testified that he was a student at Huatong Public School, 16 years old, and knew the defendant. During the summer vacation last year, because the defendant's father, Luo Zhaoxin, was assassinated, the defendant and his mother temporarily resided at my house for about a month. At 10:30 AM this morning, I received a report at school and returned home, finding two axes and the bedside cabinet under the bed opened, with

the stolen belongings. Also, the gold and diamond rings that my mother wore on her hands had been removed. Jin Lingyi also testified that she was 18 years old and a student at Xiaoming Girls' School. Three days before the incident, the defendant came and took away a leather suitcase and a radio that he had stored at our house. The radio is currently being held at the Public Security Bureau. Witness Cai Xingbao testified that he worked as a tea server at the Zhiyin Music Association downstairs at 459 North Henan Road. Around 10:00 AM on the morning of the incident, he was ordered by Wang Hefeng, a staff member of the store, to take

photographs upstairs, preparing them for Mrs. Jin (the deceased) to review. As soon as he reached the staircase, he suddenly heard Luo's groans. Suspecting she had suffered a fit, he went downstairs and returned with others, forcing the door open and discovering that the two women had been killed. He then reported to the police department. When questioned, the defendant Luo Yusheng testified that his father, Luo Zhaoxin, and the Jin family knew each other and were old acquaintances. Last year, after my father was tried, I lived at Aunt Jin's house for about a year. I only knew that

my father had two checks, each for 250 yuan, deposited in a Hangzhou bank more than ten years ago. Up to now, I can withdraw 1,000 yuan, which Aunt Jin took away. Although I asked for it, she delayed payment. I have no grievances against Aunt Jin and had no intention of harming her. Not only is there no tea server named Xu Wenxian in my school, but at 7:30 AM on the 13th, I was in the office with female teacher Xu Manqian and others revising the syllabus. At 8:00 AM, I was the master of ceremonies for the memorial week. This point

can be proven by the teachers and students in the school. As for the confession I made in the police station yesterday, it was a forced and nonsensical confession. The 100 yuan in banknotes found was borrowed from my friend Wang Zhiqing, totaling 300 yuan. After spending 200 yuan, there was still 100 yuan left, hidden in the suitcase. As for the Shanghai Bank safety deposit box number 174, it is in my own name and not Jin Dai's. At 1:30 PM on the 23rd, I went to the bank to open the box and retrieve items, including the Mainland and Shanghai

Bank passbooks and my parents' death certificates, our family's gold rings, etc. The house on Wang Mingrong's house on Huangjiaque Road was originally rented by me, with a monthly rent of 12 yuan, but it has now been subleased and all the items have been completely moved away, leaving only an empty house. I did not leave two leather suitcases at Wang Mingrong's place. This point can be confirmed by summoning the second landlord, Wang Mingrong, to identify whether it was me who sent them or someone else, etc. Finally,

the witness invited by the defendant, Xu Manqian, a female teacher, testified that she was a teacher at Mingchen Elementary School. On the morning of the incident, I was with the defendant in school opening the memorial week. He did not go out in the morning. However, regarding the defendant's testimony about the memorial week report and syllabus revision, the testimony was contradictory. Judge Liu Yu concluded the interrogation at this point, as it was already past noon, and ordered the defendant to be detained for seven days for further interrogation.

Yong'an Silver Company Case - Shen Zufuh and Others Summoned Yesterday - Yong'an Resumed Business for One Day with Shen as Manager - The Case Has Been Concluded and the Verdict Will Be Announced on the 30th 123

The case of the Yong'an Silver Company's fraudulent scheme that defrauded depositors of a large sum of money will soon reach its one-year anniversary. The case has been delayed because the responsible parties of the company have repeatedly evaded justice. So far, only the board member Lin Kanghou and board member and general manager Ou Jiancheng have been sentenced by the First Special District Court. Although the other defendants have been summoned or detained by the court, they have not been brought to justice, causing the entire case to be prolonged and difficult to resolve. Yesterday afternoon, Shen Zufuh, a native of Shaoxing and the newly appointed manager who resumed business for one day, and Dai Kechang, the manager of the Xiafei Road branch, were summoned for continued interrogation. Judge Xiao Xiefen presided over the hearing. It was investigated that the depositors of the company filed a criminal lawsuit for fraud and listed Shen and Dai as defendants. The depositors included Chen Zhongru, Zhou Shoufu, Cao Zhu, Xie Zhongying, Chen Shengyao, Gao Yiqun, Qiu Bokai, etc. The lawyers representing the plaintiffs successively stated the types of deposits and the amounts deposited. Chen Zhongru's lawyer, Lu Shaozong, solemnly stated that the 4,000 yuan deposited by Chen was completely sacrificed by Shen Zufuh. Chen only knew Shen. Shen took office as manager and asked Chen for help. Chen only deposited the money on the day of resumption. This type of deposit was called "hanging red" and was originally intended to be deposited in the morning and withdrawn in the evening, but it was eventually embezzled. Isn't this fraud, etc.? When questioned, the defendant Shen Zufuh stated that when the company first suspended business, it owed 220,000 yuan and also owed 180,000 yuan to others. Later, the board of directors decided that more than 100,000 yuan in receivables were available, so they hired me to be the manager after the resumption of business. However, on the day of resumption, the company only handed me over 20,000 yuan. The income on that day was more than 80,000 yuan, while the expenditure was more than 110,000 yuan, so it was still impossible to maintain and it suspended business again like a flash in the pan, etc. He also denied asking the plaintiff to "hang red" with the money. The court found it difficult to believe Shen's statement that he was not a shareholder of the company and was hired by the board of directors to be the manager, only responsible for business operations, etc. Therefore, they investigated what exchange conditions there were for him to serve as manager and how much he admitted to advancing. However, Shen firmly stated that he was not responsible for raising funds. Then, he stated that the company knew that he came from the banking industry and hoped that he could interact with the banking industry, so they borrowed his expertise, etc. Next, the defendant Dai Kechang stated that he used to work at the Navy Club. Ou Jiancheng knew that he had extensive social connections and an excellent reputation, so he specifically used the position of manager of the Xiafei Road branch to recruit him. Old classmates and colleagues heard that he was there and came to deposit money, about 30,000 yuan in total. The company handed over the money to the head office every day and never kept any. Unexpectedly, only nine days after taking office, the branch suspended business with the head office, so he was also a victim, etc. Then, the debate began. First, the lawyers for the plaintiffs spoke in turn. Those who included Shen and Dai in the lawsuit believed that Shen should be held responsible for fraud, saying that the company's board of directors also had a resolution that the responsibility for the second suspension should be borne by Shen. As for Dai, they requested the court to investigate and handle the case. Those whose lawsuits did not include Shen and Dai stated that the other defendants, such as Ye Hancheng and Qian Youju, could not be arrested, so they requested that the part of the case be stopped, so that it could be concluded. Finally, under the defense of the defendant's lawyer, Judge Xiao ordered Shen Zufuh to pay a bail of 3,000 yuan and wait for the verdict on September 30.

Fish Merchant Weng Zhaofang and Others Accused of Evading National Taxes - Conspiracy to Defraud during the Weighing of 50,000 Piculs of Russian Salmon - Zhu Xusheng and Others Who Conspired Confessed and Reported the Crime 124

Last winter, some people in the salted fish industry purchased 50,000 piculs of salmon from the Soviet Union Association Foreign Firm. During the weighing at the wharf, they defrauded a huge amount of 6,700 piculs, worth more than 70,000 yuan. Now, Zhu Xusheng, Chang Junfa, Zhao Lianfang and other three accomplices, considering that theft is a minor matter, but the harm to tax revenue is not insignificant, and fearing that once the incident is exposed, they will definitely be suspected as accomplices, confessed to the Municipal Public Security Bureau on July 14. They requested that it be transferred to the prosecutor's office of the District Court for investigation in accordance with the law. It is now learned that this case has been concluded after several interrogations by Prosecutor Xiao Jinying. He ordered the defendants Zhu Xusheng, Chang Junfa, Zhao Lianfang, Weng Zhaofang, Ye Zhenchang, Zheng Yunsheng, etc. to be released on bail and filed a public prosecution. Regarding the facts of the crime, the defendants Weng Zhaofang, Ye Zhenchang, and Zheng Yunsheng all opened fish shops. Last year, they purchased from the Soviet Union Association Foreign Firm. On January 6th of this year, Zhao Lianfang and the shipping clerks Ye Zhenqin and Zhang Benhua, etc., raised the carrying pole during the weighing of the fish boxes at the Yangjiadu Wharf to reduce the quantity. It is estimated that three ships in total obtained 6,700 piculs of fish, worth more than 70,000 yuan. Later, Zhu Xusheng and others divided the profits too little and informed the Municipal Public Security Bureau, which sent a letter to investigate. (Evidence and legal articles violated) The defendants jointly defrauded the Russian merchant of the salmon. According to the interrogation, Zhu Xusheng, Chang Junfa, and Zhao Lianfang described in detail how they planned to defraud. The evidence of the crime is extremely clear. They are accomplices in Article 339, paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law and should be prosecuted in accordance with the law, etc. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Judge Wu Deying specially opened the Third Court for trial. The defendants hired four lawyers, Zhang Shizhao, Zhu Yakui, Dai Ningrui, and Peng Yuanxun, to appear in court to defend them. First, Zhu Xusheng testified that last year, he purchased salmon from the Russian Assistance Association Foreign Firm through the Zhenda Foreign Firm. Because I was unemployed, Ye Zhenchang, the manager of Zhenda Foreign Firm, asked me to help when the goods arrived and told me to call the coolies. I helped greet the worker Chang Junfa and ordered me to cheat and tell the coolies not to put the fish box too firmly on the scale when weighing the fish. The rope was not completely loosened, so that the weight could be reduced. There were three ships in total. The first batch was on November 13th, totaling 37,743 boxes. The second batch was on December 23rd, totaling 43,136 boxes. The third batch was on January 6th of this year, totaling 8,129 boxes. Zhang Benhua is the shipping clerk of Zhenda. Ye Zhenchang promised to give us 20% of the profits from the fraud, but he only gave me 120 yuan. According to our calculations, the fraud amounted to more than 70,000 yuan. But I was not the only one working on the job. The people working on the scene often negotiated with me. The officer said, do you think you are getting too little, so you confessed? I replied, no, it's because I'm now repenting. The officer said, do you know you are breaking the law? I replied, I know. Because this is evading national taxes, I repent and reported it, hoping that the penalty will be reduced, etc. Next, Chang Junfa testified that he was a coolie foreman. Zhao Lianfang testified that he was a shipping clerk. The rest of the testimony was largely the same as that of Zhu Xusheng. Then, Zheng Yunsheng, Weng Zhaofang, Ye Zhenchang, Zhang Benhua, and Ye Zhenqin all testified that they denied any fraudulent activities, vaguely saying that when weighing at the wharf, there were four or five people including the impartial person, the cargo owner, and the ship escort on the scene to inspect. How could they cheat, asking for a clear understanding? The interrogating officer obtained the testimony and thought it was too late and the witnesses were not complete, so he decided not to open the debate and wait for a joint trial at a later date.

Incident of Shi Jiurong's Abduction: One Abductor Apprehended, Interrogation Postponed Awaiting Capture of Accomplices; Zhang Xiaosan Admits to Abduction Without Reservation 128

Shi Jiurong, a 32-year-old Ningbo native residing at 275 Yu Yuan Road, formerly studied mechanical engineering at the University of Michigan in the United States. After graduating, he returned to China and served as the head of the sales department at Meitong Automobile Company at 615 Avenue Foch. He used his own Buick car, license plate number 946, for transportation and employed Li Alin from Yangzhou as his chauffeur. On April 18th of this year, at 9:00 AM, Shi took his car from his residence to the Meitong Automobile Company to work. As the car arrived in front of the Meitong Automobile Company on Avenue Foch and Shi was about to get out, four kidnappers suddenly emerged from the roadside with guns. Two of the kidnappers opened the left and right rear doors of Shi's car, sat to Shi's left and right. The other two kidnappers entered the front of Shi's car, sitting next to the chauffeur and monitoring Li Alin with guns, ordering him to drive away. Li, being alert, secretly disabled the car's engine while pretending to step on the accelerator. In this critical moment, a Russian mechanic from Meitong Automobile Company happened to look up and saw Shi sitting in the car with people monitoring him, realizing something was wrong. He shouted "Robbers!" At the same time, an Indian policeman stationed there by the Public Concession to manage traffic lights also noticed the situation and rushed to Shi's car. As he inquired, the kidnappers opened fire from the car, and a bullet grazed the Indian policeman's leg. Realizing that their plan had failed, the kidnappers quickly forced Shi out of the car and fled in different directions. One kidnapper fled towards Route MAssenet, turned into Route Cardinal Mercier, and fled west and east. A Chinese constable, number 242, from the Public Concession heard the alarm and rushed to help chase after the fleeing kidnappers. The kidnapper fleeing east opened fire to resist arrest upon seeing the pursuing constable. The constable returned fire, hitting the kidnapper in the chest. The kidnapper collapsed on the side of Route Cardinal Mercier opposite number 647, dying instantly. A pistol and several bullets were found on the body. The kidnapper fleeing west also disappeared. The other two kidnappers fled west along Avenue Foch. A Western constable, McKieber, from the Jing'an Temple Police Station, happened to be patrolling on a bicycle and pursued them. The two kidnappers also opened fire to resist arrest but ultimately escaped without a trace. Afterwards, the French Concession Police Department sent detectives to take the dead robber's body to the mortuary for examination. They reported the case to the Second Special District Court, which sent officials to investigate. The body was then buried by a charitable organization. Meanwhile, the French Police Department ordered detectives to thoroughly investigate and arrest the remaining robbers. These details were reported in previous newspapers. Recently, Jin Jiulin, the Inspector General of the French Police Department, received confidential information that Zhang Xiaosan, a native of Jiangbei and an accomplice in the abduction case, was hiding on Lujiabang Road in the southern part of the city, and would pass by Rue Amiral Bayle and Route Pere Huc every morning. Inspector General Jin dispatched detectives Zhang Ziying and Zhou Buguang, along with detectives Dai Rongji, Zhu Ju, Jin Bingwen, and others, to patrol and arrest him on Rue Amiral Bayle and Route Pere Huc. After several days, at around 8:00 AM on the 24th, the informant spotted the kidnapper Zhang Xiaosan walking hurriedly north from the South Bund. The detectives swarmed forward, arrested him, and took him to the police station for interrogation. According to Zhang's confession, he admitted to conspiring to abduct Shi Jiurong, and stated that a certain person, currently at large, was the mastermind. He also identified the accomplice who was shot and killed by the police as Tian Dazhong. He was immediately ordered to be detained, and the police began to track down the remaining accomplices based on his confession. Yesterday, the police sent the robber Zhang to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court. Judge Wang Gangxu presided over the hearing. Yao Zhaodi, a lawyer from the Police Department, presented the case, stating that the investigation would take time and that the remaining accomplices needed to be arrested, requesting a postponement of the hearing. Detective Dai Rongji then reported the circumstances of the arrest of the defendant and the incident. The court verified the report and questioned the defendant, whose confession was consistent with the one given at the police station. The court then approved the postponement, ordering a reinvestigation and returning the defendant to custody.

Renji Hospital, Struggling for 91 Years, Faces Economic Difficulties Due to Economic Recession, Revenue Decreases, Deficit of Over 13,000 Yuan Last Year, Outpatient Visits Surge, Reaching 200,000 Annually 130

Renji Hospital on Shandong Road has been serving the community since the 26th year of the Daoguang reign of the Qing Dynasty (1846 AD). Its location is in McTaggart Road, with a history of 91 years. The hospital buildings have been rebuilt and expanded several times, but the location has remained the same, so those who have lived in Shanghai for a long time are familiar with "Renji Hospital in McTaggart Road". The hospital has been expanded over the years to meet the needs of the environment. Most of the funding has come from donations from enthusiastic individuals, but due to the large expenses, it has been difficult to make ends meet. Only after Henry Lester, the owner of the former Dehe Foreign Firm, provided substantial funding, was it possible to have the magnificent building standing on the south side of Shandong Road and Fuzhou Road today. From the surface, it seems that the sufficiency of its funding can be represented by this large building, but in reality, this is not entirely the case. Its need for funds is actually beyond our expectations. Since Shanghai has been shrouded in the gloomy atmosphere of economic recession, all industries have been in decline, which has had a major impact on the livelihood of society. Even if middle- and lower-class families try their best to reduce their daily needs, they still cannot make ends meet. Not to mention those who have unfortunately lost their jobs. Therefore, on the one hand, Renji Hospital is short of resources and its income has decreased, and on the other hand, demand exceeds supply, and its expenditures have increased. This phenomenon is very obvious due to the exhaustion of the social economy. In the past, middle-class families could afford a doctor, but now, due to difficult living conditions, they have no choice but to seek help from public hospitals. As for the poor and working classes, who rely on charitable hospitals for their livelihoods, their numbers have naturally increased. For this reason, the hospital is crowded with patients, and the authorities feel that they have no rice to cook. Last year, Renji Hospital had a deficit of more than 23,000 yuan in addition to various subsidies, donations, and medical expenses. The hospital, in view of the economic difficulties, has tried its best to reduce all expenses, such as the salaries of staff and workers, but the deficit still reached this number. What the hospital hopes for today is the enthusiastic donation of people from all walks of life, who are happy to donate. This is not only the beauty of feeling the pain of others and helping them, but also to create benefits for society and maintain the safety and order of the public. This principle may not be understood by the general public, especially those in the "upper class" who live in peace and comfort, and who have not paid attention to the hospitals that the working class regards as a guarantee of health, let alone pay attention to them. In fact, the occurrence of diseases, the suffering of the individual, is a small matter. If we look at it from the perspective of the family and the entire society, the impact cannot be ignored. But this is only in terms of the near-term cause and the long-term effect. Other examples, such as infectious diseases and epidemics that directly affect the public, people of the lower classes, due to their lack of knowledge and simple living conditions, are unable to prevent them in advance. It is a tragic event when they are ill and have no way to seek help and are waiting to die. Renji Hospital treats hundreds of thousands of patients every year, reducing personal suffering, curbing the spread of diseases to society, and increasing the health and happiness of people. Its contribution is truly undeniable. Let us close our eyes and think about it. Shanghai has many good doctors and hospitals with perfect equipment, but they are only for the consultation of a few people. The expensive medical expenses are as different from the copper coins of fifteen yuan charged by Renji Hospital as heaven and earth. The consultation fee of a noble person once can directly cover the outpatient expenses of hundreds of people here. But fortunately, there is this hospital, otherwise, where would these hundreds of thousands of patients go if they only had five cents of ocean? The number of daily outpatient visits to Renji Hospital is between 600 and 900. The so-called consultation fee of fifteen copper coins is only for a small number of people. Most of the patients cannot even afford the meager fifteen copper coins. Everything from diagnosis to medicine is free, which can be said to be the greatest benefit to the poor. The number of inpatients has also increased sharply recently. Due to the limited number of beds, it has not been possible to accommodate as many as possible. Ordinary patients pay six cents of ocean a day, including all food, lodging, and medical expenses, but one-third of them do not pay anything. According to people in the hospital, this six cents of ocean is only one-fifth of the total cost per patient per day. The cost of medicines is even lower. A prescription that usually costs 2.50 yuan at a pharmacy in the market only costs 25 cents of ocean in the hospital. This is just a very small example. As for the cost of abdominal surgery and other fees, which a wife cannot afford in her lifetime, the hospital performs the operation for the patient according to the needs of the patient, and charges a small fee according to the patient's ability, or waives the fee entirely for those who are extremely poor. The treatment of emergency patients, such as gunshot wounds, accidental injuries, and suicide by poisoning, is the most burdensome for Renji Hospital in the central district of the Public Concession. The efficiency of its services is also highly praised by the public. According to past statistics of the hospital, on average, every hour of the 24 hours of the day, there is an emergency patient seeking treatment, among which the number of those who commit suicide by taking poison is the most numerous. Suicide is a sin. Although the reasons are different, it is a pity that they resorted to this strategy. The physical pain is only a momentary thing for the person who commits suicide. They often muster their foolish courage to do so. As for the spiritual trauma, it cannot be expressed in physical terms. It has been seen that the hospital often earnestly exhorts those who have been saved from suicide after they have been reborn, to follow the path of happiness and destiny. This is based on the Christian spirit of saving the world, and to hope that all beings will ascend to heaven together. Renji Hospital has spacious buildings, complete equipment, quietness in the bustling city, and a not-so-bad environment. It can be called the crown of hospitals in the bustling city. The patient rooms have windows on three sides, good ventilation, and good light. There are five operating rooms, four of which are in constant use, and one is reserved for emergencies. All the equipment in them is of the latest type. The shadowless lamp on the operating table is one of its characteristics. The kitchen is located on the top of the building, using both gas and steam to prepare meals for 400 people. After the meals are cooked, they are sent to each ward by two special elevators. The completeness of its equipment is no less than that of major hospitals in Europe and the United States. The hospital has an affiliated nursing training school, which has trained a large number of nursing talents over the years. When the last graduation ceremony was held, Li Tingan, the director of the Municipal Health Bureau, and his wife personally attended the ceremony and gave words of encouragement. The current president is Dr. Patterson, and the vice president is Dr. Ferguson, who have both served in the hospital for many years. There are currently 13 foreign staff members, including six foreign female nurses. There are a total of 242 Chinese staff members, from chief physicians to nurses and workers. There are also eight physicians who work at the Lester Institute of Pathology. There is an even larger number of honorary consulting physicians outside the hospital. Renji Hospital has the largest number of outpatient visits. Seven years ago, the number was about 90,000 per year. Last year, the number of patients increased sharply to more than 183,000. Although this year has not yet reached the end of the year, it is estimated that the number will not be less than 200,000. These 200,000 outpatient visits account for almost 7% of the total population of Shanghai. It cannot be said to be a small number.

New Beijing Ship Suicide Incident on the Tongsha Ocean Surface: Young Man and Woman Jump into the Sea, Man Appears to Be Upper Class, Woman's Dress Also Modern, Jump into the Sea Together on the Outer Tongsha Ocean Surface, Male Passenger Claims to Be Wang from Shandong, Had a Sumptuous Meal Before Death 131

Datong News Agency reports that the Taikoo Company's New Beijing ship, which departed from Shanghai for Ningbo on the 23rd, had two young male and female passengers in the 19th cabin jump into the sea to commit suicide while the ship was passing through the Outer Tongsha Ocean surface. The details are as follows:

Passengers in the First-Class Cabin: The New Beijing ship departed from Shanghai for Ningbo at 5:00 PM on the 23rd. In cabin number 19 of the ship, there were two young male and female passengers. The man was about 20 years old, wearing a light gray suit. The woman was 22 years old, wearing a light green cheongsam with a white wool scarf around her neck, permed hair, and wearing openwork leather shoes. Cui Dechang, the steward of the cabin, noticed that the two passengers appeared to be upper class, so he served them diligently.

The Deceased Had a Sumptuous Meal: At about 6:00 PM that evening, the ship left the Wusong estuary, and dinner was served on the ship. Steward Cui Dechang brought in the dinner. At that time, both the man and woman had a sumptuous meal. After the meal, the two passengers took out purple grapes and candied peanuts that they had brought with them and ate them casually. At that time, the two were joking and laughing, and their relationship was very close, with no signs of world-weariness. At about 8:45 PM, the ship passed through the Outer Tongsha Ocean surface. The two passengers suddenly took off their leather shoes and changed into the straw slippers provided on the ship, saying that they were going to admire the night view of the sea on the deck.

Jumping into the Sea on the Outer Tongsha Ocean Surface: At that time, steward Cui Dechang, seeing that it was already late at night, told them to go to bed early, and the two passengers casually agreed. Before ten minutes had passed, someone suddenly shouted that someone had jumped into the sea on the aft deck. Steward Cui Dechang heard the shout and ran to the aft deck to check. Only the slippers that the two passengers were wearing were left on the stern of the ship, and the people were missing, obviously having jumped into the sea to commit suicide. He immediately reported to the captain to stop the ship and try to rescue them, but the Outer Tongsha Ocean surface was extremely vast, and there were waves at the time, so it was impossible to rescue them.

A Glimpse of the Remains: Afterwards, steward Cui Dechang checked the remains and found only the man's suit jacket, a pair of leather shoes, and the woman's pair of openwork leather shoes. There were no letters or other items. The above items have been kept by the steward and are awaiting the arrival of family members to claim them. The Datong News Agency reporter interviewed the steward Cui yesterday. According to him, the man told him during dinner that evening that he was from Shandong, surnamed Wang, and pointed to the woman and said that she was his wife. However, observing the intimate behavior of the man and woman, he was afraid that they were not officially married.

Liu Zigu's Painting Exhibition Organized by the Social Education Bureau and the Education Bureau Opened Yesterday, Wu Xingya Personally Presided Over It 132

In order to promote national painting, the Municipal Social Education Bureau and the Education Bureau jointly organized a national painting exhibition of the famous painter Mr. Liu Zigu at the Continental Commercial Building on the sixth floor, displaying more than 300 pieces of Liu's exquisite masterpieces. The details have been reported in the previous newspapers. Yesterday was the opening day, and no less than a thousand people attended the exhibition. The details of the various situations are recorded below:

Director Wu Personally Presided Over: This painting exhibition was originally intended to promote art, and it was also advocated by the Social Education Bureau and the Education Bureau, so the bureau and others sent personnel to take care of the venue. The Education Bureau sent Ding Shoutang and Shi Chongpeng, and the Social Bureau sent Zhang Binghui, Chen Binhua, etc. In addition, Director Wu also personally came to the venue to instruct everything.

A Glimpse of the Contents of the Works: All the more than 300 works are divided into two rooms for display. There are landscapes, figures, ladies, flowers, birds, orchids, and bamboos. Among them, landscapes are the most numerous. The most eye-catching ones are the Refugee Map, the Flood Map, the Mulan Joining the Army Map, and the "I Love Beauty, Not the Country" Map, which are either current events, historical facts, or allegorical, and are very valuable. Other imitations of ancient works are also very similar and can be mistaken for the real thing. The figures include the national hero Qi Jiguang's portrait, ladies such as "Qinxin Youyou", flowers and birds such as "Spring River Water Warm", and orchids and bamboos such as "Snow Bamboo, Who Does the Fragrance Reveal", which are all enough to amaze people and sigh with admiration.

Report on the Closure of the Hongkou Plague Hospital 133

The Hongkou Plague Hospital, located at the north end of Xiangyanqiao, Yucai Road, Hongkou, has been open for diagnosis and treatment since July 10th, reaching two and a half months. The results have been very good. Now that autumn has arrived and the plague is gradually subsiding, the hospital will cease outpatient services on the 25th of this month. According to the hospital's outpatient services this year, in addition to 1,459 people who were injected with preventive vaccines, a total of 8,739 cases were treated, including 1,908 cases of dysentery, 265 cases of enteritis, 875 cases of indigestion, 692 cases of gastritis, 679 cases of influenza, 556 cases of abdominal pain, 480 cases of constipation, 430 cases of gastroenteritis, 387 cases of diarrhea, 186 cases of intestinal parasites, 167 cases of malaria, 46 cases of stomach cramps, 1 case of heat stroke, and 1,167 cases of miscellaneous diseases. A total of 484 patients were hospitalized, including 6 cases of acute gastroenteritis. The medicine was ineffective, but after injecting saline, the symptoms improved greatly, and all of them were discharged safely. One patient, Bao Fuqing, was so grateful for being saved that he specially presented a plaque with the four characters "You Revived Me", which has been sent to the hospital for display. However, there were more cases of dysentery this year, with dangerous symptoms, and a total of 5 people died from the disease. One person died from heat stroke after ineffective treatment, for a total of 6 deaths. It is also known that the total expenses of the hospital this year were more than 5,430 yuan, of which more than 1,100 yuan were for medicines. This is because there were more cases of dysentery, so the cost of medicines was high, accounting for more than 20% of the total. On average, each patient cost more than 6 jiao and 2 fen, which is a reduction of one-quarter compared to the previous year.

Special Article: Opinions on the Issue of Increasing Credit Instruments (5) 142

(7) Application of New Credit Instruments in the Financial Market: The progress of the financial system is seen in the concentration of power and the flexibility of turnover, while the progress of the credit system lies in transforming stagnation into circulation. However, the so-called "progress" must still be premised on the improvement of the national economy. Therefore, although the past real estate boom in Shanghai transformed stagnation into circulation, it was not enough to be called progress.

The same is true for credit transactions. Following the old-fashioned account system leads to immediate stagnation. Therefore, changing to bill acceptance can transform stagnation into circulation. This kind of technical improvement has subtle differences on the surface, but the implications are far-reaching. It is like the steam in a kettle, which, once introduced into a steam engine, unexpectedly becomes the driving force of human civilization in an epoch-making way. At present, there are indeed many loans in China's financial industry, but due to neglect of technical improvements, the stagnant ones have not been transformed into circulation. It is believed that if we want to establish a modern credit system, we must promote the above-mentioned modern credit instruments in the following three aspects: A. Replace the current factory mortgage loans with the acceptance of corporate bonds.

B. Replace the current movable property mortgage loans with bank acceptance drafts. C. Discount commercial acceptance drafts to replace the current credit loans. While the money supply is not yet relaxed, it is not possible to play a larger role in the corporate bond aspect in one fell swoop. However, for the sake of promotion, each bank can immediately select companies with outstanding credit, advise them to issue bonds, and accept them themselves. At the same time, they can cooperate with the Chinese Business Securities Exchange to make a public auction, so that the bonds can circulate in the market, and the industrial securities market can be established. In the future, anyone who requests a loan secured by a factory mortgage will be planned for the issuance of corporate bonds. When banks accept corporate bonds, although they also have to pay the same funds, after the bonds are auctioned on the exchange, they can gradually flow into the hands of general investors. Since transactions have an official market price, it is not difficult to obtain financial accommodation through mortgages in times of urgency. This is very different from the current stagnant factory mortgage loans.

Regarding the promotion of bank acceptance drafts, the Joint Preparatory Committee of the Bankers Association has jointly established a bill acceptance office. The method is that industrial and commercial entrepreneurs who need financing provide collateral to the office. After the office approves it, they can issue drafts for the office to accept. These acceptance drafts can be purchased or discounted by each bank. Applicants for acceptance can use it to obtain financial accommodation. After banks purchase or discount these drafts, they can still sell or rediscount them to obtain financial accommodation when they need funds themselves. Therefore, bank acceptance drafts can be listed as secondary reserves in peacetime, and their liquidity is very different from that of current mortgage loans.

Commercial acceptance drafts are currently being strongly promoted by the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce. The silk and satin industry and the electrical machinery and silk weaving industry associations have already implemented them first. The method is that when industrial and commercial entrepreneurs sell goods on credit, unlike the current method of only registering accounts after receiving a reply, making it a kind of stagnant account receivable, they instead use the procedure of issuing drafts and having the buyer accept them, making it a negotiable receivable. After acceptance, the draft can be discounted at a financial institution to obtain financial accommodation. After the financial institution discounts the draft, it can also obtain financial accommodation through rediscounting when needed. Therefore, in various Western countries, commercial acceptance drafts have also become the second reserve of the financial industry. Compared with the current credit loans, which are both dangerous and extremely stagnant, it is truly a world apart.

After the financing methods of the financial industry are transformed according to the above three aspects, the abnormal development of the long-term capital market can be gradually shifted, the industrial securities market can be established, and the short-term capital market can be completely rationalized and modernized. The result is that, in addition to turning stagnation into circulation, the financing of long-term capital is made public due to the issuance of industrial securities, and the financing of short-term capital can also be used to observe the general trend of expansion and contraction from the acceptance and rediscount amounts, prevent problems before they occur, and obtain accurate targets. Compared with the current financing of each doing its own thing and not consulting each other, which leads to unlimited credit expansion and accelerated cycles of panic, the progress is not to be compared with reason. (To be continued)

Words of Contribution

The National Products Industry and the Revival of Industry and Commerce 144

— Yang An

Credit Instruments and Knowledge of Final Accounts

There are two major issues in the National Products industry that should be urgently addressed, namely the (1) opinions on the issue of increasing credit instruments and (2) knowledge of final accounts for industrial and commercial institutions, published by the Committee for the Revival of Industry and Commerce. These two issues have been discussed by the committee's sub-group several times before being presented to society. Our National Products industry should earnestly accept and diligently study them, so as to open a new record in future business operations.

(1) The insufficiency of credit instruments has been unanimously recognized by the Chinese people. The fact that the majority of our National Products industry can operate businesses worth hundreds of thousands of yuan with tens of thousands of yuan of capital is entirely dependent on credit instruments. Now, with the tightening of finance and the reduction of the use of credit instruments, the impact on our National Products industry is the greatest. Now that the Committee for the Revival of Industry and Commerce has made contributions to expanding credit instruments, our National Products industry should sincerely cooperate with the financial industry and implement (1) replacing the current factory mortgage loans with the acceptance of corporate bonds, (2) replacing the current movable property mortgage loans with bank acceptance drafts, and (3) replacing the current credit loans with the discounting of commercial acceptance drafts. Before implementation, it is especially necessary to study management, strengthen strength, refine products, and reduce costs, so as to gain the trust of the financial industry and comrades who wholeheartedly promote national products. Otherwise, if the content is corrupt and the business is declining, any facility will be futile and useless. This is one thing that the National Products industry should pay attention to.

(2) The handling of final accounts by industrial and commercial institutions is the most important undertaking, but the procedures handled by the industrial and commercial sectors have always been inadequate. For example, the provision of depreciation, the preparation of bad debts, the making of dividends as expenses, the inclusion of customer accounts in the cash balance, and various bills are all inappropriate in strict terms. Now the Committee for the Revival of Industry and Commerce can pay attention to this and invite accounting experts to agree on a copy of the knowledge of handling final accounts, showing accounting staff the way to go and the standards that should be followed. This is of great benefit to national product factories. It is hoped that the authorities of each factory will pay attention to and implement it quickly, so as to sweep away the troubles of the previous confusion accounts. It is not difficult to handle final accounts, but it is difficult to fit the accounting system and the principle of fairness. This is the second thing to pay attention to.

The above-mentioned is extremely important. If the people can have no demands on others and give full play to the spirit of doing their best, then the one line of vitality in the National Products industry will belong to this.

The Crisis of Massive Imports of Luxury Goods 145

— Xuan Wan

Everyone knows that China's huge trade deficit in recent years is a fatal injury to the bankruptcy of our entire national economy. However, the term "trade deficit" seems too general and needs to be analyzed in detail, because China is a country with very backward industries. Therefore, in the entire trade deficit, there are also many machines and materials that are necessary for the development of national products. We must certainly make good use of this kind of thing to improve the current production and promote the Chinese economy to a completely self-sufficient stage.

However, what I want to point out in particular here is that in the entire trade deficit, there is a crisis of massive imports of luxury goods over the years, and the luxury goods I am talking about here include all perfumes, rouge, cosmetics, real and fake jewelry, cigarettes, cigars, various wines, soda, candy, shark fins, bird's nests, etc. In the present situation of poverty and exhaustion of wealth, there should no longer be such a huge consumption, but facts speak louder than words. For example, during the National Products Year for Women last year, it was discovered that more than one million yuan of cosmetics were imported, which caused great controversy. Even this year, when the market is becoming increasingly lifeless and the business of national product factories is becoming more difficult, newspapers tell us that imports of cosmetics are still pouring in. According to statistics, it has only decreased by 15% compared to last year. I think no one can be satisfied with this and feel that the future of the National Products Movement still requires greater efforts!

Moreover, I recently saw an article by Mr. Gu Yuantian in the Economic Weekly of the Ta Kung Pao, "The Awareness We Should Have Regarding Reducing the International Trade Deficit," which included a comparative table of the value of luxury goods and the value of the trade deficit since 1934. According to his statistics, the value of luxury goods over these many years accounts for more than 22% of the total value of the trade deficit, which shows that the amount of luxury goods consumed by the Chinese people is really alarming. Although it is said that a part of it is consumed by foreign residents in China, the quantity will never be so large. China is still in an era of such backward industries, but it has such a large consumption, which is a most terrible phenomenon. If the Chinese people can recognize the difficulties of the times earlier, and everyone is willing to save and work hard to produce and build, and turn all the trade deficit of luxury goods into productive products such as machinery and materials; then I think the development of the Chinese economy would have made considerable achievements long ago. But the Chinese people are going against the grain, which gives us such a serious feeling and requires everyone to urgently find ways to make greater efforts in the National Products Movement and the Thrift Movement to save it.

We know that the consumers of luxury goods are mostly the urban bourgeoisie, who have a wealth of knowledge. Now that the country has reached such a state, you can all wake up!

Yixing Kiln and Huishan Clay 146

— Rong Yu

When you go to people's houses to see, the teapots and teacups they use are of Western goods for the superior ones, and Japanese goods for the secondary ones. When asked why they don't use Chinese goods, they say in unison: "Jiangxi goods are too expensive, and they are not exquisite at all! I remember when I was a child, the toys I played with were always made of clay, such as 'Big Afu,' 'Wenchang,' and 'God of Wealth.' I made vows like Buddha with a few little partners, and it was quite interesting. Now the things that children play with are not right, what Western dolls! Rubber animals! Toy guns! It's really all kinds of things, much more interesting than before. It's a pity that most of these things are not quasi-national products." These two feelings made me think of "Yixing Kiln" and "Huishan Clay," so I will briefly describe some opinions below:

Yixing is a county in Jiangsu Province, and the mud produced there is fine, clean, and very viscous, so it is considered a good material for making kiln embryos. The kiln households in this area specialize in making teapots and teacups, so Yixing teapots can also be considered famous all over the world. The color of the mud is purple-red, so the things that are fired are also this color, antique and charming, which is also lovely. If the fine things are topped with a layer of wonderful color, then red, yellow, blue, and white can be made at will. I think the teapots and teacups produced in Yixing are not outdated, but unfortunately, the workers who make them now still stick to the old methods, so the production is slow and the cost is high. If scientific methods are used to increase the rate, and specialized talents are used to improve them, I am afraid that Yixing teapots and teacups will surpass foreign goods. I hope that the local kiln households will work hard soon!

Speaking of Huishan clay sculptures, they were also famous all over the country in the past, and every child had a "Big Afu" to play with. Since the advent of new-style toys, this "Big Afu" has been in the ranks of being overthrown. This is also not their fault. First, Big Afu is clumsy and ugly, and second, it is broken when touched. Now many workers who sculpt clay figures also know how to improve it, what models! What Liu, Guan, and Zhang's three knots of justice! All kinds of new patterns are sculpted. However, these things can only get the taste of general lower-level people, and upper-middle-class families rarely buy them for display. I think if we improve it further, and imitate the method of sculpting plaster statues in the West, we can sculpt half-length portraits of famous people from ancient and modern times with mud, or heroes, or beauties, all painted with powder and not colored. This can also win the favor of people who love beauty!

Although the above two things are small productions, if they are improved and promoted, they are also a strange soldier in the National Products industry!

— Li Jialu

The Dark Horse of the Domestic Rubber Industry 150

— Kang Sheng

Since the rubber industry in our country rose in 1928 and was at its peak, it has recently shown a trend of overall collapse. The reasons for this are nothing more than the devaluation and dumping of foreign goods and the bankruptcy of the rural economy. However, the biggest reason for its failure is that the goods do not know how to improve, the management is not refined, and the rough manufacturing has ruined the reputation. As a result, the market is shrinking, sales are decreasing, and turnover is difficult, so it has become a situation where the mountain rain is about to come and the wind is filling the building.

In this rubber industry, the only one who can strive for survival, be self-reliant, and be the pillar in the middle of the stream is the Zhengtian Xinji Factory, the creator of Warrior sneakers. In the past, Zhengtian Factory was famous throughout the country for its Dasheng brand overshoes, running shoes, and sneakers. The quality was excellent, and everyone knew it, so it was known as the "old general in shoes." After reorganizing Xinji, it sought further advancement and worked hard for revival. With a long-term vision and strong perseverance, it eliminated all inferior products and decided to use high-quality raw materials, the latest technology, and scientific management to create crystallized products that meet modern purchasing principles. Warrior sneakers are especially the outstanding products of the factory. Since its launch, it has still been able to make a name for itself even in this fragmented and depressed market. This phenomenon is really the price of the factory's efforts. The factory has also established a mail-order department a year ago to serve customers from afar to benefit the remote areas. Wherever there is a post office, you can directly write to purchase and enjoy the products of the factory. As for the rapid delivery, free postage and remittance fees, and the guarantee that the goods sent are perfect, it is meticulous and can be favored by customers from afar. Recently, there have also been ways to arouse users' interest and connect users' feelings, offering rewards to solicit methods, humbly seeking the advancement of business. It is truly the dark horse of the domestic rubber industry.

Hot-selling National Velvet Yarn 151

The Shangyu Minguo National Goods Wool Yarn Company, organized by various renowned velvet yarn shops on Xingsheng Street, has recently produced two types of products: "Double Hand" brand and "Double Ocean" brand. They are soft, vividly colored, inexpensive, and of high quality. They are no less than imported goods. As a result, various merchant groups and managers are vying to order in advance, creating a situation where supply cannot meet demand. Due to the daily increase in sales and significant sacrifices, the company will slightly increase prices from January 1st to protect its capital. Furthermore, in the shortest period, they will launch the highest quality and most upscale "Chrysanthemum" brand velvet yarn to meet the needs of society.

Designated Routes for Private Cars During the National Games 159

The Sixth National Games, scheduled to be held at the Municipal Sports Field in the city center starting on Double Tenth Day, has been reported earlier. The Municipal Government Assistance Temporary Office, in order to avoid traffic congestion due to the concentration of public and private cars on the main roads leading to the city center during the Games, has consulted with the Public Works Bureau to establish temporary vehicle routes. The following is an excerpt regarding private cars: (Vehicle routes during the National Games) 2. Private cars going to the city center from the concession and Zhabei: A. Vehicles from the eastern district should enter through Yangshupu, take Jungong Road, pass Wuquan Road, the Municipal Government, Sanmin Road, and go to the northern parking lot of the Sports Field. B. Vehicles from the Hongkou district should take North Sichuan Road, pass Jiangwan Road, West Sports Association Road, Xiangyin Road, Songhu Road, and go to the northern parking lot of the Sports Field. C. Vehicles can also take North Henan Road, pass Duoshan Road, Jiangwan Road, West Sports Association Road, Xiangyin Road, Songhu Road, and go to the northern parking lot of the Sports Field. D. Vehicles from the western district should take Zhongshan Road, pass West Baoxing Road, Shuidian Road, Xiangyin Road, Songhu Road, and go to the northern parking lot of the Sports Field. Returning from the city center to Zhabei and the concession: A. From the northern parking lot of the Sports Field, take Funan Right Road, Xiangyin Road (eastbound to Jungong Road) or westbound via Huangxing Road, enter Ningguo Road. After 8:00 PM, change to Qimei Road and enter Dixiwei Road. B. From the northern parking lot of the Sports Field, pass Funan, Wuquan Road, enter Jungong Road, and go to Yangshupu. (Parking lot management rules) (Regarding private cars) The northern parking lot between Songhu Road and Funan Right Road at the Sports Field is designated for black-plated private cars. 1. The northern parking lot is divided into seventeen "parking zones," numbered from north to north seventeen. A. Zones North 1 to North 7 are for the eastern area, specifically for vehicles taking Jungong Road. B. Zones North 8 to North 17 are for the western area, specifically for vehicles taking Songhu Road. (To facilitate command, vehicles are prohibited from entering at the east entrance of Xiangyin Road and the entrance of Yinxianggang Town). 2. Each parking zone is marked with a wooden pole. 3. Each parking zone will have a wooden sign indicating the number of vehicles that can be parked in that zone. 4. Vehicles must be parked according to the designated zone. 5. Passengers of private cars must disembark after the vehicle has parked in the appropriate parking zone and walk to the Sports Field. Disembarking on Songhu Road is strictly prohibited. 6. Private cars must wait for the owner to board at the parking lot and must not drive elsewhere to pick them up. Those who do not wish to stay should immediately leave the city center.

Dear Sir,

After reading the newspaper, we learned that the Guangdong swimming team has some questions regarding the selection of swimming athletes in Shanghai. The swimming selection committee feels the need to respond. When the committee announced the call for city-wide participation in the preliminary selection and training, Wen Jingling did not register and did not participate in any of the training sessions. If he were allowed to be an athlete from this city simply because of his past achievements, those swimmers who trained on time every day and whose performance was equal to Wen would inevitably feel regretful for being eliminated. Furthermore, even if the committee allowed Wen to be an athlete, it is questionable whether Wen himself would be willing to serve Shanghai, as he has never expressed his opinion. Wen gave up voluntarily and was not eliminated. As for Xu Jun, he also did not register to participate in swimming. His most proficient event is volleyball. At the joint meeting of the Shanghai selection committees, it was generally agreed that athletes should develop their specialties and should not participate in multiple events. It has not yet been determined which unit Xu Jun will represent during the selection, so he was not selected. As for the diving performance, the committee specially invited Mr. Bai Li, the YMCA sports director, to assist in order to ensure fairness and accuracy. Mr. Bai did not know any of the participants and judged the performances based on the merits of their posture, being fair and impartial. We hereby declare, Ling Xitao and Peng Sanmei

World Heavyweight Boxing Champion Baer Loses to Joe Louis, Falls in the Fourth Round and Cannot Get Up 166

(Havas News Agency, New York, 24th) The famous American boxer Baer, the world heavyweight boxing champion last year, was once defeated by Braddock in June of this year. He recently held a match with black boxer Joe Louis at Yankee Stadium, with as many as 90,000 spectators. The two fought until the fourth round, when Baer fell and could not get up, and was quite badly injured. The intensity of the battle was rare since he started boxing. According to reports, Joe Louis had the upper hand in the first round, because Baer did not follow the advice of the previous famous boxer, "Po Sai," and only adopted a weak offensive against Joe Louis, which allowed Joe Louis to take advantage of the situation. Under a fierce attack, Baer was immediately injured and bled. By the second round, Baer's movements were sluggish, allowing Joe Louis to dominate all the way. In the third round, the two fought fiercely again, but Baer still did not show any strength. Finally, he was knocked down by Joe Louis and struggled to get up after nine seconds. But in the fourth round, Baer finally couldn't hold on and fell, unable to get up again. The referee announced Joe Louis's victory, and the whole stadium was astonished.

(Nanjing, 25th) The Ministry of Education has formulated two types of statistical tables for middle school and normal school student graduation examinations for the 23rd year. On the 25th, it issued a notice to all departments, requiring them to report to the Ministry one month after receiving the document.

Ministry of Education Plans to Formulate Preferential Admission Measures for Descendants of Sages (Nanjing, 25th) The Ministry of Education plans to formulate preferential admission measures for descendants of sages. In all public and private schools in Qufu, Zou County, and Jiaxiang counties, all descendants of the Four Sages will be exempted from tuition fees. Before the start of the school year, the local education administrative organs will be responsible for reporting to the Ministry, and the central government will subsidize education fees. The Ministry of Education will order the Shandong Education Department to comply.

Ministry of Education Orders the Implementation of Educational Broadcasting Methods Using Radio 169

On the 24th, the Ministry of Education issued a notice to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities, stating: "Upon investigation, the implementation of educational broadcasting using radio has been previously ordered to the factories concerned to urge affiliated schools and halls to install educational equipment. Now, the preparations of this Ministry have gradually progressed, and broadcasting is scheduled to begin on the tenth festival of this year. The outline of service methods for radio receiving instructors in various provinces by the Education Plant Bureau, the guidelines for middle schools to use educational broadcasting, and the guidelines for public education halls to use educational broadcasting are hereby issued. The said department is ordered to comply and inform the affiliated schools and halls accordingly." This order.

Outline of Service Methods for Radio Receiving Instructors in Education Departments and Bureaus of Various Provinces and Cities

1. This outline is formulated based on the provisions of page 9 of the National Training Class for Radio Receiving Instructors in Secondary Schools and Public Education Halls. 2. The tasks of radio receiving instructors (hereinafter referred to as instructors) in education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities are as follows: (1) Promote the value of educational broadcasting so that students and the public can truly understand it. (2) Guide secondary schools and public education halls in various provinces and cities regarding the installation and repair of radio receivers and their receiving methods. (3) Guide the above schools and halls in effectively communicating the content of educational broadcasting to the audience. (4) Examine the achievements of the above schools and halls in using educational broadcasting. 3. Instructors may request the competent education department or bureau to pre-purchase an appropriate number of radios and spare parts for the installation of various schools and halls. 4. Instructors shall, one month after the end of each semester, prepare a detailed report in duplicate on the work situation and the general situation of educational broadcasting in each school and hall, and submit it to the competent education department or bureau, one of which shall be forwarded by the said department or bureau to this Ministry for review. 5. Instructors are directly affiliated staff of the Education Department or Bureau. Those who work in affiliated institutions shall be transferred to work in this institution by the said department or bureau after the promulgation of these measures. 6. The number of instructors in each province and city may be determined by the education departments and bureaus of each province and city according to actual needs, and the names, ages, birthplaces, experiences, and academic qualifications shall be reported to the Ministry for review. 7. These measures shall be implemented after promulgation.

Guidelines for Middle Schools to Use Educational Broadcasting

1. Middle schools shall organize an educational broadcasting promotion committee to plan and implement the following matters: (1) Plan the addition or improvement of radio receiving equipment and listening places. (2) Plan teaching materials or teaching aids related to broadcasting topics for students to use when listening (such as maps, forms, charts, specimens, instruments, objects to help understanding, and other teaching materials, etc.). (3) Appoint teachers related to the topic to guide students in taking notes, and after each broadcast, give students a concise explanation of the main points of the broadcast. (4) Study other methods of using educational broadcasting. 2. The educational broadcasting promotion committee shall consist of the director of studies (or director of guidance), the director of moral education, and teachers of various subjects. The director of studies (or director of education) shall be the chairman of the committee. 3. Each school shall inform or issue to students in advance the schedule, topics, outlines, times, and teaching materials of the Ministry regarding educational broadcasting. 4. Each educational broadcast shall be treated as a formal one-hour class. Each school shall supervise students to listen on time and prepare attendance books for roll call. 5. When holding examinations in each subject, the content of the broadcast related to each subject shall be appropriately included in the questions of the relevant subjects. 6. Teachers of each subject shall be responsible for grading students' broadcast notes related to their subjects. 7. This "Guidelines" shall be formulated and issued by the Ministry to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities for distribution to affiliated middle schools for compliance.

Guidelines for Public Education Halls to Use Educational Broadcasting

. Public education halls shall organize an educational broadcasting promotion committee to plan and implement the following matters: (1) Study methods to encourage the public to listen. (2) Plan the addition or improvement of radio receiving equipment and listening places. (3) Plan teaching materials or teaching aids related to broadcasting topics for the convenience of the public to use when listening (such as maps, forms, charts, specimens, instruments, words or objects to help understanding, and other teaching aids, etc. (4) Appoint instructors to use teaching materials or teaching aids during educational broadcasting time to guide the audience to understand the content of the broadcast. After each broadcast, give the audience a concise explanation of the main points of the broadcast. (5) Study other methods of using educational broadcasting. 2. The educational broadcasting promotion committee shall be composed of the director of the public education hall, the section chief of the competent education administrative organ, (the county public education hall shall be composed of the director or section chief of the education bureau), the president of the education association, representatives of local legal public organizations, and a number of enthusiastic educators. The director of the public education hall shall be the chairman of the committee. 3. Public education halls shall inform or issue to the public in advance the schedule, topics, outlines, times, and teaching materials of the Ministry regarding educational broadcasting. 4. Public education halls must try to attract listeners before each educational broadcast and arouse their interest in continuing to listen. 5. After each educational broadcast, public halls shall post a summary of the broadcast content in appropriate places inside and outside the hall to attract public attention. 6. Public education halls shall, within one month after the end of the semester, report to the competent education administrative organ the work process and improvement suggestions of using educational broadcasting in the semester. 7. This "Guidelines" shall be formulated and issued by the Ministry to the education administrative organs of various provinces and cities for distribution to affiliated public education halls for violation.
